\doxysubsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} is a special \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Channel}{Channel}} that acts as the main entry point into the logging framework.

An application uses instances of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} class to generate its log messages and send them on their way to their final destination. \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} instances are organized in a hierarchical, tree-\/like manner and are maintained by the framework. Every \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} object has exactly one direct ancestor, with the exception of the root logger. A newly created logger inherits its properties -\/ channel and level -\/ from its direct ancestor. Every logger is connected to a channel, to which it passes on its messages. Furthermore, every logger has a log level, which is used for filtering messages based on their priority. Only messages with a priority equal to or higher than the specified level are passed on. For example, if the level of a logger is set to three (P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR), only messages with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL and P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+A\+T\+AL will propagate. If the level is set to zero, the logger is effectively disabled.

The name of a logger determines the logger\textquotesingle{}s place within the logger hierarchy. The name of the root logger is always \char`\"{}\char`\"{}, the empty string. For all other loggers, the name is made up of one or more components, separated by a period. For example, the loggers with the name H\+T\+T\+P\+Server.\+Request\+Handler and H\+T\+T\+P\+Server.\+Listener are descendants of the logger H\+T\+T\+P\+Server, which itself is a descendant of the root logger. There is not limit as to how deep the logger hierarchy can become. Once a logger has been created and it has inherited the channel and level from its ancestor, it loses the connection to it. So changes to the level or channel of a logger do not affect its descendants. This greatly simplifies the implementation of the framework and is no real restriction, because almost always levels and channels are set up at application startup and never changed afterwards. Nevertheless, there are methods to simultaneously change the level and channel of all loggers in a certain hierarchy.

There are also convenience macros available that wrap the actual logging statement into a check whether the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is sufficient to actually log the message. This allows to increase the application performance if many complex log statements are used. The macros also add the source file path and line number into the log message so that it is available to formatters. Variants of these macros that allow message formatting with \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacePoco_acde2b5aff4f0d67961e2eeb394542bb0}{Poco\+::format()}} are also available. Up to four arguments are supported.

Examples\+: poco\+\_\+warning(logger, \char`\"{}\+This is a warning\char`\"{}); poco\+\_\+information\+\_\+f2(logger, \char`\"{}\+An informational message with args\+: \%d, \%d\char`\"{}, 1, 2); 

Definition at line 38 of file Logger.\+h.

Returns a reference to the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} with the given name. If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}} does not yet exist, it is created, based on its parent logger.

W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: This method is not thread safe. You should probably use \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger_a76f8a4d2fd0037126b2e6c9501fa14c9}{get()}} instead. The only time this method should be used is during program initialization, when only one thread is running. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classPoco_1_1Logger_a06dc63fd382c826c7c0cfe2108ef7752}\label{classPoco_1_1Logger_a06dc63fd382c826c7c0cfe2108ef7752}}

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+UG and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+A\+T\+AL, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+F\+A\+T\+AL and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{information()}{information()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/13]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Poco\+::\+Logger\+::information (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{fmt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{value1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+I\+ON, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+I\+ON and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

% FIG 62
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classPoco_1_1Logger_a31ba06703cd44ec93b7f515d1c5200a0}\label{classPoco_1_1Logger_a31ba06703cd44ec93b7f515d1c5200a0}} 
\index{Poco::Logger@{Poco::Logger}!is@{is}}
\index{is@{is}!Poco::Logger@{Poco::Logger}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{is()}{is()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Poco\+::\+Logger\+::is (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{level }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Logs the given message, followed by the data in buffer.

The data in buffer is written in canonical hex+\+A\+S\+C\+II form\+: Offset (4 bytes) in hexadecimal, followed by sixteen space-\/separated, two column, hexadecimal bytes, followed by the same sixteen bytes as A\+S\+C\+II characters. For bytes outside the range 32 .. 127, a dot is printed.

Sets or changes a configuration property.

Only the \char`\"{}channel\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}level\char`\"{} properties are supported, which allow setting the target channel and log level, respectively, via the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1LoggingRegistry}{Logging\+Registry}}. The \char`\"{}channel\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}level\char`\"{} properties are set-\/only. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Channel_aeafdcc5ce2e0e38d96f15a60a563da4e}{Poco\+::\+Channel}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Poco\+::\+Logger\+::notice (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{fmt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Any}{Any}} \&}]{value1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+CE, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+I\+CE and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

Sets the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level using a symbolic value.

Valid values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item none (turns off logging)
\item fatal
\item critical
\item error
\item warning
\item notice
\item information
\item debug
\item trace 
\end{DoxyItemize}

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1File}{File}} must be a static string, such as the value of the {\bfseries{F\+I\+LE}} macro. The string is not copied internally for performance reasons. ~\newline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Poco\+::\+Logger\+::warning (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{msg,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char $\ast$}]{file,  }\item[{int}]{line }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Logger}{Logger}}\textquotesingle{}s log level is at least P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classPoco_1_1Message}{Message}} with priority P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG and the given message text and sends it to the attached channel.

\doxysubsection{Field Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classPoco_1_1Logger_adecb49d80885ebcf125c60b8be392160}\label{classPoco_1_1Logger_adecb49d80885ebcf125c60b8be392160}} 
\index{Poco::Logger@{Poco::Logger}!ROOT@{ROOT}}
\index{ROOT@{ROOT}!Poco::Logger@{Poco::Logger}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ROOT}{ROOT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} std\+::string Poco\+::\+Logger\+::\+R\+O\+OT\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Parses a symbolic log level from a string and returns the resulting numeric level.

Valid symbolic levels are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item none (turns off logging)
\item fatal
\item critical
\item error
\item warning
\item notice
\item information
\item debug
\item trace
\end{DoxyItemize}

The level is not case sensitive.
